| <span data-ttu-id="36aa2-463">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="36aa2-463">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="36aa2-464">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="36aa2-464">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="36aa2-1664">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="36aa2-1664">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="36aa2-1665">A classe **MS-DFSR-Connection** faz parte do suporte ao serviço de replicação do sistema de arquivos distribuído (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="36aa2-1665">The **ms-DFSR-Connection** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
